# Dialog Log

This file records interactive dialog between the **user** and **Claude Code** for this project.

It is intended as a chronological, append-only audit log:
- Each entry is timestamped (with timezone).
- User input and Claude responses are clearly labeled.
- New dialog entries are appended below the â€œLatest Dialogâ€ section.
- Older entries follow in chronological order.

This file may be updated automatically by local tooling.
It is not part of the public project history and may be excluded from the main branch.

[38;2;255;255;255mâº[39m I've reviewed the CLAUDE.md file. This is the OpenCV Pipeline Editor project - a JavaFX-based graphical node editor for building OpenCV image processing pipelines.

  Key points I'll follow:
  - [1mNo commits without explicit approval[22m - I'll suggest commits but wait for you to test and confirm
  - [1mNo claiming fixes work[22m - I'll say "I've made changes, please test" rather than asserting something is fixed
  - [1mBuild with [38;2;177;185;249mmvn compile[22m[39m to catch errors after changes

  The project also includes work on [1mccwrap[22m - a Python wrapper for Claude Code that adds journaling to DIALOG.md, email notifications when awaiting input, and Gmail polling for remote replies.

  What would you like to work on?
